This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements
    :adl
    :action-costs
    :typing
    :negative-preconditions
 )
 (:types
  agent
  location
  receptacle
  object
  rtype
  otype
  )

 (:predicates
    (atLocation ?a - agent ?l - location)
    (receptacleAtLocation ?r - receptacle ?l - location)
    (objectAtLocation ?o - object ?l - location)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (inReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (isReceptacleObject ?o - object)
    (inReceptacleObject ?innerObject - object ?outerObject - object)
    (isReceptacleObjectFull ?o - object)
    (wasInReceptacle ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (checked ?r - receptacle)
    (examined ?l - location)
    (inspectedObject ?o - object)
    (inspectedAgent ?a - agent)
    (receptacleType ?r - receptacle ?t - rtype)
    (canContain ?rt - rtype ?ot - otype)
    (objectType ?o - object ?t - otype)
    (holds ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (holdsAny ?a - agent)
    (holdsAnyReceptacleObject ?a - agent)
    (full ?r - receptacle)
    (isClean ?o - object)
    (cleanable ?o - object)
    (isHot ?o - object)
    (heatable ?o - object)
    (isCool ?o - object)
    (coolable ?o - object)
    (pickupable ?o - object)
    (moveable ?o - object)
    (toggleable ?o - object)
    (isOn ?o - object)
    (isToggled ?o - object)
    (sliceable ?o - object)
    (isSliced ?o - object)
 )

  (:functions
    (distance ?from ?to)
    (total-cost) - number
   )

(:action look
    :parameters (?a - agent ?l - location)
    :precondition
        (and
            (atLocation ?a ?l)
        )
    :effect
        (and
            (examined ?l)
        )
)

(:action inventory
    :parameters (?a - agent)
    :effect
        (and
            (inspectedAgent ?a)
        )
)

(:action examineReceptacle
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition
        (and
            (exists (?l - location)
                (and
                    (atLocation ?a ?l)
                    (receptacleAtLocation ?r ?l)
                )
            )
        )
    :effect
        (and
            (checked ?r)
        )
)

(:action examineObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object)
    :precondition
        (or
            (exists (?l - location ?r - receptacle)
                (and
                    (atLocation ?a ?l)
                    (receptacleAtLocation ?r ?l)
                    (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                    (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
              )
            )
            (holds ?a ?o)
        )
    :effect
        (and
            (inspectedObject ?o)
        )
)

(:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?a - agent ?lStart - location ?lEnd - location ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
                    (atLocation ?a ?lStart)
                    (receptacleAtLocation ?r ?lEnd)
                  )
    :effect (and
                (not (atLocation ?a ?lStart))
                (atLocation ?a ?lEnd)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
 )

(:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?l - location ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
            (openable ?r)
            (atLocation ?a ?l)
            (receptacleAtLocation ?r ?l)
            (not (opened ?r))
            )
    :effect (and
                (opened ?r)
                (checked ?r)
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
 )

(:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?l - location ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
            (openable ?r)
            (atLocation ?a ?l)
            (receptacleAtLocation ?r ?l)
            (opened ?r)
            )
    :effect (and
                (not (opened ?r))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
 )

 (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?l - location ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition
        (and
            (pickupable ?o)
            (atLocation ?a ?l)
            (receptacleAtLocation ?r ?l)
            (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
            (not (holdsAny ?a))
            (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
        )
    :effect
        (and
            (not (inReceptacle ?o ?r))
            (holds ?a ?o)
            (holdsAny ?a)
            (not (objectAtLocation ?o ?l))
            (increase (total-cost) 1)
        )
 )

 (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?l - location ?o - object ?r - receptacle ?ot - otype ?rt - rtype)
    :precondition (and
            (holds ?a ?o)
            (atLocation ?a ?l)
            (receptacleAtLocation ?r ?l)
            (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r))
            (objectType ?o ?ot)
            (receptacleType ?r ?rt)
            (canContain ?rt ?ot)
            )
    :effect (and
                (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
                (objectAtLocation ?o ?l)
                (not (holds ?a ?o))
                (not (holdsAny ?a))
                (increase (total-cost) 1)
            )
 )

 (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?l - location ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    :precondition (and
            (cleanable ?o)
            (receptacleType ?r SinkBasinType)
            (atLocation ?a ?l)
            (receptacleAtLocation ?r ?l)
            (holds ?a ?o)
            )
    :effect (and
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
                (isClean ?o)
            )
 )

 (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?l - location ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    :precondition (and
            (heatable ?o)
            (receptacleType ?r MicrowaveType)
            (atLocation ?a ?l)
            (receptacleAtLocation ?r ?l)
            (holds ?a ?o)
            )
    :effect (and
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
                (isHot ?o)
                (not (isCool ?o))
            )
 )

 (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?l - location ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    :precondition (and
            (coolable ?o)
            (receptacleType ?r FridgeType)
            (atLocation ?a ?l)
            (receptacleAtLocation ?r ?l)
            (holds ?a ?o)
            )
    :effect (and
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
                (isCool ?o)
                (not (isHot ?o))
            )
 )

 (:action ToggleObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?l - location ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and
            (toggleable ?o)
            (atLocation ?a ?l)
            (receptacleAtLocation ?r ?l)
            (inReceptacle ?o ?r)
            )
    :effect (and
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
                (when (isOn ?o)
                    (not (isOn ?o)))
                (when (not (isOn ?o))
                    (isOn ?o))
                (isToggled ?o)
            )
 )

 (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?l - location ?co - object ?ko - object)
    :precondition
            (and
                (sliceable ?co)
                (or
                    (objectType ?ko KnifeType)
                    (objectType ?ko ButterKnifeType)
                )
                (atLocation ?a ?l)
                (objectAtLocation ?co ?l)
                (holds ?a ?ko)
            )
    :effect (and
                (increase (total-cost) 5)
                (isSliced ?co)
            )
 )

(:action help
    :parameters (?a - agent)
    :effect
        (and
            (inspectedAgent ?a)
        )
)

)

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types agent receptacle object sharpObject microwaveReceptacle sinkbasinReceptacle fridgeReceptacle)
 (:predicates
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holds ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (microwaveReceptacle ?r - receptacle)
    (sinkbasinReceptacle ?r - receptacle)
    (fridgeReceptacle ?r - receptacle)
    (sharpObject ?o - object)
    (cleanable ?o - object)
    (isClean ?o - object)
    (heatable ?o - object)
    (isHot ?o - object)
    (coolable ?o - object)
    (isCool ?o - object)
    (sliceable ?o - object)
    (isSliced ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
 )
 (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?a ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
 )
 (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (not (holds ?a ?o)) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holds ?a ?o))

    (opened ?r - receptacle)

    (sharpObject ?o - object)
    (cleanable ?o - object)

    (heatable ?o - object)
    (isHot ?o - object)

    (isSliced ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
 )
 (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?a ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
 )

    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)

            :action GotoLocation

        2. open a receptacle if it is closed

        3. close a receptacle
            :action CloseObject
            :parameters (?r - receptacle)

        10. slice an object using a sharp object
            :action SliceObject
            :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)

            If necessary, use the PickupObject action to retrieve the item, and the GotoLocation action to move to the correct place.

            Hint: 
            1. If you want to heat, clean, and cool an object, after you go to that aim receptacle, do not put the object in the receptacle but do the action directly. For example, go to fridge, then cool the object with receptacle.

            3. If you want to examine or look at an object with a lamp, you should first go to the receptacle where the object is located and then pick it up and take the USE action of the lamp. You don't need to take the lamp but directly use it.
            4. If there are multiple actions needed to complete the task, you can break them down into smaller subgoals. For example, if you need to slice and then heat an object, first focus on slicing it, and then move on to heating it.

        In summary, the first stage is all about finding the object—this might involve going to an unvisited receptacle and opening it if necessary.

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :action-costs :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types 
    agent 
    object 
    receptacle 
    sharpObject - object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
 )
 (:predicates
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holds ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (cleanable ?o - object)
    (isClean ?o - object)
    (heatable ?o - object)
    (isHot ?o - object)
    (coolable ?o - object)
    (isCool ?o - object)
    (sliceable ?o - object)
    (isSliced ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
 )
 (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?a - agent ?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at ?a ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at ?a ?from)) (at ?a ?to))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
 )
 (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (openable ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r) (not (holds ?a ?o)) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holds ?a ?o))
 )
 (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (holds ?a ?o)) (in ?o ?r))
 )
 (:action useObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (in ?o ?r))
    :effect (used ?o)
 )
 (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - microwaveReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (isHot ?o)
 )
 (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - sinkbasinReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (isClean ?o)
 )
 (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?o - object ?r - fridgeReceptacle)
    :precondition (and (holds ?a ?o) (at ?a ?r))
    :effect (isCool ?o)
 )
 (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?a - agent ?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - sharpObject)
    :precondition (and (at ?a ?r) (holds ?a ?sharp_o) (in ?co ?r) (sliceable ?co))
    :effect (and (isSliced ?co) (not (holds ?a ?sharp_o)) (in ?sharp_o ?r))
 )
)

 )

(define (domain alfred)
 (:requirements :adl :typing :negative-preconditions)
 (:types 
    agent 
    object 
    receptacle 
    sharpObject - object
    microwaveReceptacle - receptacle
    sinkbasinReceptacle - receptacle
    fridgeReceptacle - receptacle
 )
 (:predicates
    (at ?a - agent ?r - receptacle)
    (openable ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (in ?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    (holds ?a - agent ?o - object)
    (cleanable ?o - object)
    (isClean ?o - object)
    (heatable ?o - object)
    (isHot ?o - object)
    (coolable ?o - object)
    (isCool ?o - object)
    (sliceable ?o - object)
    (isSliced ?o - object)
    (used ?o - object)
 )
 (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (at agent1 ?from)
    :effect (and (not (at agent1 ?from)) (at agent1 ?to))
 )
 (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at agent1 ?r) (openable ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
 )
 (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at agent1 ?r) (openable ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
 )
 (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at agent1 ?r) (in ?o ?r) (not (holds agent1 ?o)) (or (not (openable ?r)) (opened ?r)))
    :effect (and (not (in ?o ?r)) (holds agent1 ?o))
 )

    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
